### Development Step 3: Find Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski‚Äôs Character in ‚ÄòMagda M.‚Äô via Cast and Filmography Search

**Description**: Search for information about the actor Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski's role in the production 'Magda M.' to identify which character he played. Focus on finding cast information, filmography details, or production records through multiple search approaches: (1) Search for 'Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski Magda M. cast character role', (2) Look for Polish film/TV databases or IMDb entries for 'Magda M.' production, (3) Search for Kasprzykowski's complete filmography to identify his role in 'Magda M.', (4) Check Polish entertainment sources or production company information about 'Magda M.' casting. Extract the character name he portrayed in this production to complete the task.

**Use Cases**:
- Entertainment database enrichment and automated character role extraction for actor profiles in online movie encyclopedias
- Journalism fact-checking of actor filmography details and character roles when preparing articles on Polish television series
- Academic film studies research and metadata gathering for analyzing casting patterns in early-2000s TV dramas
- Streaming service content catalog automation and cast-to-character mapping to ensure accurate credits in user interfaces
- Localization and dubbing preparation by extracting original character names for translating subtitles and scripts
- AI chatbot integration for on-demand actor role lookups when users ask ‚ÄúWho did Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski play in Magda M.?‚Äù
- Archival library cataloging and verification of cast roles in historical television productions for media heritage projects

```
import os
import re
import requests

# Search for information about Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski's role in 'Magda M.'
query = 'Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski Magda M. cast character role'
max_results = 15
type = "search"

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print(f"Searching Google for: {query}")
print(f"Max results: {max_results}")
print(f"Search type: {type}")

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": max_results,
"type": type,
}

# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
print("\nSearch request successful!")

# Save raw results to workspace for inspection
import json
with open('workspace/kasprzykowski_magda_m_search_results.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"Raw search results saved to: workspace/kasprzykowski_magda_m_search_results.json")

# Process and display results
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"\nFound {len(results['organic_results'])} organic search results:")
print("=" * 60)

for i, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"\nResult {i}:")
print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"URL: {link}")
print(f"Snippet: {snippet}")

# Check for relevant keywords in title and snippet
combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower()
relevant_keywords = ['kasprzykowski', 'magda m', 'cast', 'character', 'role', 'actor', 'film', 'series']
found_keywords = [kw for kw in relevant_keywords if kw in combined_text]

if found_keywords:
print(f"*** RELEVANT KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_keywords)} ***")

# Look for potential character names in snippets
# Common patterns: "plays [character]", "as [character]", "role of [character]"
character_patterns = [
r'plays?\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'as\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'role\s+of\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'character\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'wcieli≈Ç\s+siƒô\s+w\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'gra\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
]

for pattern in character_patterns:
matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text, re.IGNORECASE)
if matches:
print(f"*** POTENTIAL CHARACTER NAME(S) FOUND: {matches} ***")

print("-" * 40)
else:
print("\nNo organic search results found.")
else:
print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")

print("\nInitial search completed. Results saved to workspace for further analysis.")

### Development Step 2: Post-1977 20th-Century Malko Competition Winners and Their Nationalities (Including Defunct States)

**Description**: Search for comprehensive information about the Malko Competition, focusing on identifying all recipients from the 20th Century after 1977. Target these research approaches: (1) Official Malko Competition website or archives for complete winner lists, (2) Classical music databases and competition records, (3) Music journalism sources and historical archives, (4) Academic or institutional music resources. Extract complete recipient data including names, years of victory, and recorded nationalities. Pay special attention to nationalities that correspond to countries that no longer exist (such as USSR, Yugoslavia, Czechoslovakia, East Germany, etc.). Compile a systematic list of all post-1977 20th century winners with their nationality information for further analysis.

**Use Cases**:
- Archiving and extracting grant awardees from a foundation‚Äôs online records (2000‚Äì2020) to analyze funding trends by recipient nationality
- Aggregating hackathon winner data from multiple tech event websites post-2015 for corporate sponsorship decision support
- Mining patent award information from USPTO HTML archives to map inventor nationalities and identify innovation hotspots
- Automating extraction of sanctioned entities from government PDF/HTML sanction lists to keep compliance databases up to date
- Building a music streaming service feature that compiles historical competition winners and their nationalities for curated playlists
- Parsing academic conference websites to index keynote speakers and their affiliations for university library catalogs
- Extracting sports tournament champions from archived sports federation pages to feed a real-time analytics dashboard for media outlets

import json

print("Objective: Extract specific winner names, years (1978-2000), and nationalities from saved sources\n")

print(f"Files in workspace: {len(workspace_files)}")
for file in workspace_files:
print(f" - {file}")
else:
print("No workspace directory found")
exit()

# First, let's inspect the research summary to understand what we have
summary_file = 'workspace/malko_research_summary.json'
if os.path.exists(summary_file):
print(f"\n=== INSPECTING RESEARCH SUMMARY ===\n")

with open(summary_file, 'r') as f:
summary_data = json.load(f)

# Inspect the structure of the summary
print("Summary file structure:")
for key, value in summary_data.items():
if isinstance(value, list):
print(f" {key}: List with {len(value)} items")
elif isinstance(value, dict):
print(f" {key}: Dictionary with keys: {list(value.keys())}")
else:
print(f" {key}: {value}")

print(f"\nSuccessful sources found: {len(summary_data['sources_data'])}")

for key, value in source.items():
print(f" {key}: {value}")

# Identify the main Wikipedia file to analyze

for source in summary_data.get('sources_data', []):

break

print("This should contain the detailed winner information")
else:
print("\nNo Wikipedia file identified")
else:
print(f"Research summary file not found: {summary_file}")

# Now let's inspect any analysis files that were created
analysis_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.startswith('malko_analysis')]
print(f"\n=== INSPECTING ANALYSIS FILES ===\n")
print(f"Found {len(analysis_files)} analysis files")

for analysis_file in analysis_files:
print(f"\nAnalyzing: {analysis_file}")

print("Analysis file structure:")
for key, value in analysis_data.items():
if isinstance(value, list):
print(f" {key}: List with {len(value)} items - {value[:5]}...") # Show first 5 items
elif isinstance(value, str) and len(value) > 100:
print(f" {key}: String with {len(value)} characters - First 100: {value[:100]}...")
else:
print(f" {key}: {value}")

### Development Step 2: Locate Actor Who Voiced Ray in Polish Version of Everybody Loves Raymond

**Description**: Search for information about the Polish-language version of 'Everybody Loves Raymond' to identify the actor who played the character Ray. Focus on finding cast information, dubbing details, or Polish adaptation records through multiple search approaches: (1) Search for 'Everybody Loves Raymond Polish version cast Ray actor', (2) Look for Polish television adaptation or dubbing information, (3) Search Polish entertainment databases or Wikipedia pages about the show's international versions, (4) Check for any Polish remake or localized version details. Extract the complete name of the actor who voiced or played Ray in the Polish version for further analysis.

**Use Cases**:
- Localization QA for dubbing studios: automatically extract and verify voice actor names and character mappings for the Polish adaptation of a US sitcom to ensure accurate credits.
- Streaming service metadata enrichment: aggregate cast and adaptation details for ‚ÄúEverybody Loves Raymond‚Äù Polish version and other localized shows to improve content discoverability and search accuracy.
- Academic research in cross-cultural media studies: compile and compare actor and character information from multiple international versions to analyze localization and naming conventions.
- Entertainment news portal content automation: update articles with real-time information on new local adaptations and voice-cast changes for trending TV series across global markets.
- Digital library catalog enhancement: enrich catalog entries with detailed cast data from international remakes to boost user browsing, recommendations, and cross-referencing of related content.
- DVD/Blu-ray packaging and marketing asset generation: generate precise cast listings and localized credits for inclusion in physical product inserts and promotional materials.
- Fan wiki database maintenance: automate extraction and validation of character‚Äìactor relationships in localized shows to keep community-driven encyclopedias and fan sites up to date.

from ddgs import DDGS import json import os # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print('Created workspace directory') else: print('Workspace directory already exists') print('=== DISTINCTIVE INTERNATIONAL ARAB FESTIVALS AWARDS 2022 RESEARCH ===\n') print('Objective: Find Pakistani actresses who received awards at the 2022 Dubai festival sponsored by Algedra\n') # Search Strategy 1: Direct search for the specific festival and Pakistani actresses query1 = 'Distinctive International Arab Festivals Awards 2022 Dubai Algedra Pakistani actresses winners' print(f'Search 1: {query1}') print('Searching for specific festival information with Pakistani actresses...') searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) results1 = searcher.text( query1, max_results=15, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yandex", "brave", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) print(f'Search 1 completed. Found {len(results1)} results.') # Save first search results with open('workspace/arab_festivals_search1.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results1, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print('Search 1 results saved to: workspace/arab_festivals_search1.json\n') # Analyze first search results if results1: print('=== SEARCH 1 RESULTS ANALYSIS ===') for i, result in enumerate(results1, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\nResult {i}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'URL: {url}') print(f'Description: {body}') # Check for relevant keywords combined_text = f'{title} {body}'.lower() relevant_keywords = ['distinctive', 'arab festivals', 'awards', '2022', 'dubai', 'algedra', 'pakistani', 'actress', 'winner'] found_keywords = [kw for kw in relevant_keywords if kw in combined_text] if found_keywords: print(f'*** RELEVANT KEYWORDS FOUND: {", ".join(found_keywords)} ***') # Look for Pakistani actress names or award categories if any(term in combined_text for term in ['pakistani', 'actress', 'award', 'winner', 'honored']): print('*** POTENTIALLY RELEVANT FOR PAKISTANI ACTRESSES ***') print('-' * 50) else: print('No results found for Search 1') print('\n' + '='*70) print('SEARCH 1 COMPLETED - PROCEEDING TO SEARCH 2') print('='*70) # Search Strategy 2: Focus on official festival announcements query2 = '"Distinctive International Arab Festivals Awards" 2022 Dubai official announcement Pakistani' print(f'\nSearch 2: {query2}') print('Searching for official festival announcements...') results2 = searcher.text( query2, max_results=15, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yandex", "brave", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) print(f'Search 2 completed. from ddgs import DDGS import json import os # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print('Created workspace directory') else: print('Workspace directory already exists') print('=== DISTINCTIVE INTERNATIONAL ARAB FESTIVALS AWARDS 2022 RESEARCH - PHASE 2 ===') print('Objective: Fix variable scoping issue and complete comprehensive search analysis\n') # First, let's inspect the existing search results from Phase 1 print('=== INSPECTING EXISTING SEARCH RESULTS ===') search1_file = 'workspace/arab_festivals_search1.json' if os.path.exists(search1_file): print(f'Found existing search results: {search1_file}') # Inspect the file structure first with open(search1_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search1_data = json.load(f) print(f'Search 1 data type: {type(search1_data)}') print(f'Number of results: {len(search1_data) if isinstance(search1_data, list) else "Not a list"}') if isinstance(search1_data, list) and len(search1_data) > 0: print('Sample result structure:') sample_result = search1_data[0] print(f'Keys in first result: {list(sample_result.keys()) if isinstance(sample_result, dict) else "Not a dict"}') # Now analyze all results with proper variable scoping print('\n=== ANALYZING SEARCH 1 RESULTS (FIXED) ===') pakistani_actresses_info = [] for i, result in enumerate(search1_data, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\nResult {i}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'URL: {url}') print(f'Description: {body}') # Fix: Define combined_text within the loop scope combined_text = f'{title} {body}'.lower() relevant_keywords = ['distinctive', 'arab festivals', 'awards', '2022', 'dubai', 'algedra', 'pakistani', 'actress', 'winner'] found_keywords = [kw for kw in relevant_keywords if kw in combined_text] if found_keywords: print(f'*** RELEVANT KEYWORDS FOUND: {", ".join(found_keywords)} ***') # Look for Pakistani actress names or award categories if any(term in combined_text for term in ['pakistani', 'actress', 'award', 'winner', 'honored']): print('*** POTENTIALLY RELEVANT FOR PAKISTANI ACTRESSES ***') pakistani_actresses_info.append({ 'result_number': i, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'description': body, 'found_keywords': found_keywords }) print('-' * 50) print(f'\nFound {len(pakistani_actresses_info)} potentially relevant results for Pakistani actresses') else: print('No existing search results found, will perform fresh searches') pakistani_actresses_info = [] print('\n' + '='*70) print('CONTINUING WITH SEARCH 2 AND 3') print('='*70) # Search Strategy 2: Focus on Algedra sponsorship and 2022 ceremony query2 = 'Algedra Interior Design "Distinctive International Arab Festivals Awards" 2022 ceremony Pakistani actresses' print(f'\nSearch 2: {query2}') print('Searching for Algedra-sponsored ceremony with Pakistani actresses...') searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) results2 = searcher.text( query2, max_results=15, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yandex", "brave", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) print(f'Search 2 completed. from ddgs import DDGS import json import os # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print('Created workspace directory') else: print('Workspace directory already exists') print('=== DISTINCTIVE INTERNATIONAL ARAB FESTIVALS AWARDS 2022 RESEARCH - PHASE 4 ===') print('Objective: Completely resolve scoping issues and complete comprehensive search analysis\n') # First, let's inspect the existing search results from previous phases print('=== INSPECTING EXISTING SEARCH RESULTS ===') search1_file = 'workspace/arab_festivals_search1.json' if os.path.exists(search1_file): print(f'Found existing search results: {search1_file}') # Load and inspect the file structure with open(search1_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search1_data = json.load(f) print(f'Search 1 data type: {type(search1_data)}') print(f'Number of results: {len(search1_data) if isinstance(search1_data, list) else "Not a list"}') if isinstance(search1_data, list) and len(search1_data) > 0: print('Sample result structure:') sample_result = search1_data[0] print(f'Keys in first result: {list(sample_result.keys()) if isinstance(sample_result, dict) else "Not a dict"}') # Now analyze all results with completely restructured approach to avoid scoping issues print('\n=== ANALYZING SEARCH 1 RESULTS (RESTRUCTURED TO AVOID SCOPING) ===') pakistani_actresses_info = [] # Define keywords outside the loop relevant_keywords = ['distinctive', 'arab festivals', 'awards', '2022', 'dubai', 'algedra', 'pakistani', 'actress', 'winner'] pakistani_terms = ['pakistani', 'actress', 'award', 'winner', 'honored'] for i, result in enumerate(search1_data, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\nResult {i}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'URL: {url}') print(f'Description: {body}') # Create combined text for analysis combined_text = f'{title} {body}'.lower() # Find keywords using a simple approach to avoid scoping issues found_keywords = [] for keyword in relevant_keywords: if keyword in combined_text: found_keywords.append(keyword) if found_keywords: print(f'*** RELEVANT KEYWORDS FOUND: {", ".join(found_keywords)} ***') # Check for Pakistani actress relevance using simple approach is_pakistani_relevant = False for term in pakistani_terms: if term in combined_text: is_pakistani_relevant = True break if is_pakistani_relevant: print('*** POTENTIALLY RELEVANT FOR PAKISTANI ACTRESSES ***') pakistani_actresses_info.append({ 'search': 1, 'result_number': i, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'description': body, 'found_keywords': found_keywords }) print('-' * 50) print(f'\nSearch 1 Analysis Complete: Found {len(pakistani_actresses_info)} potentially relevant results for Pakistani actresses') else: print('No existing search results found, starting fresh') pakistani_actresses_info = [] search1_data = [] print('\n' + '='*70) print('PERFORMING SEARCH 2: ALGEDRA SPONSORSHIP FOCUS') print('='*70) # Search Strategy 2: Focus on Algedra sponsorship and 2022 ceremony query2 = 'Algedra Interior Design "Distinctive International Arab Festivals Awards" 2022 ceremony Pakistani actresses' print(f'\nSearch 2: {query2}') print('Searching for Algedra-sponsored ceremony with Pakistani actresses...') searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) results2 = searcher.text( query2, max_results=15, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yandex", "brave", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) print(f'Search 2 completed. Found {len(results2)} results.') # Save second search results with open('workspace/arab_festivals_search2.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results2, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print('Search 2 results saved to: workspace/arab_festivals_search2.json') # Analyze second search results with restructured approach if results2: print('\n=== SEARCH 2 RESULTS ANALYSIS ===') # Define terms outside the loop official_terms = ['official', 'press release', 'announcement', 'ceremony', 'winners list'] award_terms = ['best actress', 'outstanding', 'achievement', 'recognition', 'honored'] pakistani_terms_s2 = ['pakistani', 'pakistan', 'actress'] for i, result in enumerate(results2, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\nResult {i}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'URL: {url}') print(f'Description: {body}') # Create combined text for analysis combined_text = f'{title} {body}'.lower() # Check for official sources using simple approach has_official_content = False for term in official_terms: if term in combined_text: has_official_content = True break if has_official_content: print('*** POTENTIAL OFFICIAL SOURCE ***') # Check for award information using simple approach has_award_content = False for term in award_terms: if term in combined_text: has_award_content = True break if has_award_content: print('*** POTENTIAL AWARD CATEGORY INFORMATION ***') # Check for Pakistani content using simple approach has_pakistani_content = False for term in pakistani_terms_s2: if term in combined_text: has_pakistani_content = True break if has_pakistani_content: print('*** CONTAINS PAKISTANI ACTRESS INFORMATION ***') pakistani_actresses_info.append({ 'search': 2, 'result_number': i, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'description': body }) print('-' * 50) else: print('No results found for Search 2') print('\n' + '='*70) print('PERFORMING SEARCH 3: ENTERTAINMENT NEWS FOCUS') print('='*70) # Search Strategy 3: Focus on news coverage and entertainment reports query3 = '"Pakistani actresses" awards Dubai 2022 "Arab Festivals" entertainment news' print(f'\nSearch 3: {query3}') print('Searching for entertainment news coverage of Pakistani actresses at Arab festivals...') results3 = searcher.text( query3, max_results=15, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yandex", "brave", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) print(f'Search 3 completed. Found {len(results3)} results.') # Save third search results with open('workspace/arab_festivals_search3.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results3, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print('Search 3 results saved to: workspace/arab_festivals_search3.json') # Analyze third search results with restructured approach if results3: print('\n=== SEARCH 3 RESULTS ANALYSIS ===') # Define terms outside the loop actress_indicators = ['actress', 'actor', 'performer', 'artist', 'celebrity'] award_indicators = ['award', 'winner', 'honored', 'recognized', 'achievement', 'best', 'outstanding'] for i, result in enumerate(results3, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\nResult {i}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'URL: {url}') print(f'Description: {body}') # Create combined text for analysis combined_text = f'{title} {body}'.lower() # Find actress terms using simple approach found_actress_terms = [] for term in actress_indicators: if term in combined_text: found_actress_terms.append(term) # Find award terms using simple approach found_award_terms = [] for term in award_indicators: if term in combined_text: found_award_terms.append(term) if found_actress_terms and found_award_terms: print(f'*** ACTRESS + AWARD CONTENT: {found_actress_terms} + {found_award_terms} ***') # Check for Pakistani content if 'pakistan' in combined_text or 'pakistani' in combined_text: print('*** PAKISTANI CONTENT DETECTED ***') pakistani_actresses_info.append({ 'search': 3, 'result_number': i, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'description': body, 'actress_terms': found_actress_terms, 'award_terms': found_award_terms }) print('-' * 50) else: print('No results found for Search 3') print('\n' + '='*70) print('COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH ANALYSIS COMPLETED') print('='*70) # Save comprehensive analysis analysis_summary = { 'search_objective': 'Find Pakistani actresses who received awards at Distinctive International Arab Festivals Awards 2022 in Dubai sponsored by Algedra', 'searches_performed': [ {'query': 'Distinctive International Arab Festivals Awards 2022 Dubai Algedra Pakistani actresses winners', 'results_count': len(search1_data)}, {'query': query2, 'results_count': len(results2)}, {'query': query3, 'results_count': len(results3)} ], 'total_results': len(search1_data) + len(results2) + len(results3), 'pakistani_actress_relevant_results': len(pakistani_actresses_info), 'relevant_results_details': pakistani_actresses_info, 'files_created': [ 'arab_festivals_search1.json', 'arab_festivals_search2.json', 'arab_festivals_search3.json', 'arab_festivals_comprehensive_analysis.json' ] } with open('workspace/arab_festivals_comprehensive_analysis.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(analysis_summary, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print('\nFINAL SUMMARY:') print(f'- Total searches performed: 3') print(f'- Total results collected: {analysis_summary["total_results"]}') print(f'- Results potentially relevant to Pakistani actresses: {len(pakistani_actresses_info)}') print(f'- Analysis saved to: workspace/arab_festivals_comprehensive_analysis.json') # Display key findings if pakistani_actresses_info: print('\n=== KEY FINDINGS FOR PAKISTANI ACTRESSES ===') for idx, finding in enumerate(pakistani_actresses_info, 1): print(f'\nFinding {idx} (from Search {finding["search"]}):') print(f'Title: {finding["title"]}') print(f'URL: {finding["url"]}') print(f'Description: {finding["description"]}') else: print('\n*** NO SPECIFIC PAKISTANI ACTRESS INFORMATION FOUND IN CURRENT SEARCHES ***') print('This may indicate:') print('1. The specific 2022 ceremony may not have featured Pakistani actresses') print('2. Information may be in non-English sources') print('3. More specific search terms may be needed') print('4. The event details may not be widely documented online') print('\nAll search data saved for detailed examination of specific Pakistani actress award recipients.')

import os
import re
import requests
import json

# Search for Polish version of 'Everybody Loves Raymond' cast information
print('=== SEARCHING FOR POLISH VERSION OF EVERYBODY LOVES RAYMOND ===')
print('Task: Find the actor who played Ray in the Polish-language version')
print()

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Warning: Missing SERPAPI_API_KEY. Will attempt search anyway...")
print()

# Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist
workspace_dir = 'workspace'
os.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)

# Search approach 1: Direct search for Polish cast information
print('--- SEARCH 1: Polish version cast information ---')
query1 = 'Everybody Loves Raymond Polish version cast Ray actor'
print(f'Searching: {query1}')

params1 = {
"q": query1,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 10,
"type": "search",
}

response1 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params1)
print(f'API response status: {response1.status_code}')

if response1.status_code == 200:
results1 = response1.json()

# Save results to workspace
with open('workspace/raymond_polish_search1.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results1, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
print('Results saved to workspace/raymond_polish_search1.json')

if results1.get("organic_results"):
print(f'Found {len(results1["organic_results"])} results')

# Analyze results for cast information
for i, result in enumerate(results1['organic_results'], 1):
print(f'\n--- Result {i} ---')
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
url = result.get('link', 'No URL')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f'Title: {title}')
print(f'URL: {url}')
print(f'Snippet: {snippet}')

# Look for Polish-related keywords
combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower()
polish_indicators = ['polish', 'polska', 'poland', 'dubbing', 'voice', 'actor']
found_indicators = [ind for ind in polish_indicators if ind in combined_text]

if found_indicators:
print(f'*** POLISH-RELATED: Found keywords: {found_indicators} ***')
else:
print('No organic results found')
else:
print(f'Search 1 failed: {response1.status_code} - {response1.text}')

print('\n' + '='*60)

# Search approach 2: Polish television dubbing
print('--- SEARCH 2: Polish television dubbing ---')
query2 = '"Everybody Loves Raymond" polish television dubbing voice actors'
print(f'Searching: {query2}')

params2 = {
"q": query2,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 10,
"type": "search",
}

response2 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params2)
print(f'API response status: {response2.status_code}')

if response2.status_code == 200:
results2 = response2.json()

# Save results to workspace
with open('workspace/raymond_polish_search2.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results2, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
print('Results saved to workspace/raymond_polish_search2.json')

if results2.get("organic_results"):
print(f'Found {len(results2["organic_results"])} results')

# Analyze results for dubbing information
for i, result in enumerate(results2['organic_results'], 1):
print(f'\n--- Result {i} ---')
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
url = result.get('link', 'No URL')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f'Title: {title}')
print(f'URL: {url}')
print(f'Snippet: {snippet}')

# Look for actor names or dubbing information

dubbing_indicators = ['voice', 'actor', 'cast', 'dubbing', 'ray', 'raymond']

}

# Save results to workspace

**Description**: Search for information about the Polish-language version of 'Everybody Loves Raymond' to identify the actor who played the character Ray. Focus on finding cast information, dubbing details, or Polish adaptation records through multiple search approaches: (1) Search for 'Everybody Loves Raymond Polish version cast Ray actor', (2) Look for Polish television adaptation or dubbing information, (3) Search Polish entertainment databases or Wikipedia pages about the show's international versions, (4) Check for any Polish remake or localized version details. Extract the complete name of the actor who voiced or played Ray in the Polish version for further analysis.

**Use Cases**:
- Localization QA for dubbing studios: automatically extract and verify voice actor names and character mappings for the Polish adaptation of a US sitcom to ensure accurate credits.
- Streaming service metadata enrichment: aggregate cast and adaptation details for ‚ÄúEverybody Loves Raymond‚Äù Polish version and other localized shows to improve content discoverability and search accuracy.
- Academic research in cross-cultural media studies: compile and compare actor and character information from multiple international versions to analyze localization and naming conventions.
- Entertainment news portal content automation: update articles with real-time information on new local adaptations and voice-cast changes for trending TV series across global markets.

import os
import json

# Based on the tester's feedback, we found the key information:
# Polish adaptation called 'Wszyscy kochajƒÖ Romana' (Everybody Loves Roman)
# Actor: Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski plays the Ray character (Roman)

print('=== ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS FOR POLISH RAYMOND ACTOR ===')
print('Based on tester feedback: Found Polish adaptation and the actor name')
print()

# Let's examine the most promising search result file first
search3_file = 'workspace/raymond_polish_search3.json'

if os.path.exists(search3_file):
print(f'Examining {search3_file} (Wikipedia search results)...')

with open(search3_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
search3_data = json.load(f)

print(f'File structure keys: {list(search3_data.keys())}')

if 'organic_results' in search3_data:
print(f'Number of organic results: {len(search3_data["organic_results"])}')

# Look for the specific result about 'Wszyscy kochajƒÖ Romana'
for i, result in enumerate(search3_data['organic_results'], 1):
title = result.get('title', '')
url = result.get('link', '')
snippet = result.get('snippet', '')

print(f'\n--- Result {i} Analysis ---')
print(f'Title: {title}')
print(f'URL: {url}')
print(f'Snippet: {snippet}')

# Check if this is the key result about the Polish adaptation
if 'Wszyscy kochajƒÖ Romana' in title:
print('*** KEY FINDING: This is the Polish adaptation page! ***')
print('Extracting actor information...')

# The snippet should contain the actor name
if 'Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski' in snippet:
print('\nüéØ ACTOR IDENTIFIED: Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski')
print('This actor plays the Ray character (Roman) in the Polish version')

**Description**: Search for information about the actor Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski's role in the production 'Magda M.' to identify which character he played. Focus on finding cast information, filmography details, or production records through multiple search approaches: (1) Search for 'Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski Magda M. cast character role', (2) Look for Polish film/TV databases or IMDb entries for 'Magda M.' production, (3) Search for Kasprzykowski's complete filmography to identify his role in 'Magda M.', (4) Check Polish entertainment sources or production company information about 'Magda M.' casting. Extract the character name he portrayed in this production to complete the task.

**Use Cases**:
- Entertainment database enrichment and automated character role extraction for actor profiles in online movie encyclopedias
- Journalism fact-checking of actor filmography details and character roles when preparing articles on Polish television series
- Academic film studies research and metadata gathering for analyzing casting patterns in early-2000s TV dramas
- Streaming service content catalog automation and cast-to-character mapping to ensure accurate credits in user interfaces
- Localization and dubbing preparation by extracting original character names for translating subtitles and scripts
- AI chatbot integration for on-demand actor role lookups when users ask ‚ÄúWho did Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski play in Magda M.?‚Äù
- Archival library cataloging and verification of cast roles in historical television productions for media heritage projects

```
import os
import re
import requests

# Search for information about Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski's role in 'Magda M.'
query = 'Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski Magda M. cast character role'
max_results = 15
type = "search"

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print(f"Searching Google for: {query}")
print(f"Max results: {max_results}")
print(f"Search type: {type}")

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": max_results,
"type": type,
}

# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
print("\nSearch request successful!")

# Save raw results to workspace for inspection
import json
with open('workspace/kasprzykowski_magda_m_search_results.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"Raw search results saved to: workspace/kasprzykowski_magda_m_search_results.json")

# Process and display results
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"\nFound {len(results['organic_results'])} organic search results:")
print("=" * 60)

for i, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"\nResult {i}:")
print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"URL: {link}")
print(f"Snippet: {snippet}")

# Check for relevant keywords in title and snippet
combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower()
relevant_keywords = ['kasprzykowski', 'magda m', 'cast', 'character', 'role', 'actor', 'film', 'series']
found_keywords = [kw for kw in relevant_keywords if kw in combined_text]

if found_keywords:
print(f"*** RELEVANT KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_keywords)} ***")

# Look for potential character names in snippets
# Common patterns: "plays [character]", "as [character]", "role of [character]"
character_patterns = [
r'plays?\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'as\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'role\s+of\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'character\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'wcieli≈Ç\s+siƒô\s+w\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'gra\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
]

for pattern in character_patterns:
matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text, re.IGNORECASE)
if matches:
print(f"*** POTENTIAL CHARACTER NAME(S) FOUND: {matches} ***")

print("-" * 40)
else:
print("\nNo organic search results found.")
else:

Import DuckDuckGo search from ddgs import DDGS import time # Initialize searcher searcher = DDGS(timeout=10) # Search 1: Direct Maya Ali debut search print('--- SEARCH 1: Maya Ali debut 2012 ---') query1 = 'Maya Ali debut 2012 first drama series Pakistani actress' print(f'Searching: {query1}') try: results1 = searcher.text(query1, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us") if results1: print(f'Found {len(results1)} results') # Save results with open('workspace/maya_ali_debut_ddg_search1.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results1, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print('Results saved to workspace/maya_ali_debut_ddg_search1.json') # - Entertainment database enrichment and automated character role extraction for actor profiles in online movie encyclopedias
- Journalism fact-checking of actor filmography details and character roles when preparing articles on Polish television series
- Academic film studies research and metadata gathering for analyzing casting patterns in early-2000s TV dramas

- Archival library cataloging and verification of cast roles in historical television productions for media heritage projects

```
import os
import re
import requests

# Search for information about Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski's role in 'Magda M.'
query = 'Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski Magda M. cast character role'
max_results = 15
type = "search"

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print(f"Searching Google for: {query}")
print(f"Max results: {max_results}")
print(f"Search type: {type}")

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": max_results,
"type": type,
}

# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
print("\nSearch request successful!")

# Save raw results to workspace for inspection
import json
with open('workspace/kasprzykowski_magda_m_search_results.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"Raw search results saved to: workspace/kasprzykowski_magda_m_search_results.json")

# Process and display results
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"\nFound {len(results['organic_results'])} organic search results:")
print("=" * 60)

for i, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"\nResult {i}:")
print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"URL: {link}")
print(f"Snippet: {snippet}")

# Check for relevant keywords in title and snippet
combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower()
relevant_keywords = ['kasprzykowski', 'magda m', 'cast', 'character', 'role', 'actor', 'film', 'series']
found_keywords = [kw for kw in relevant_keywords if kw in combined_text]

if found_keywords:
print(f"*** RELEVANT KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_keywords)} ***")

# Look for potential character names in snippets
# Common patterns: "plays [character]", "as [character]", "role of [character]"
character_patterns = [
r'plays?\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'as\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'role\s+of\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'character\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'wcieli≈Ç\s+siƒô\s+w\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'gra\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
]

for pattern in character_patterns:

if matches:
print(f"*** POTENTIAL CHARACTER NAME(S) FOUND: {matches} ***")

print("-" * 40)
else:

### Development Step 1: Goldfinger (1964) Finale Concealment Objects and Colors Used by Bond and Pussy Galore

**Description**: Search for detailed information about the ending of the 1964 James Bond film 'Goldfinger' starring Sean Connery. Focus specifically on the final scenes where James Bond and Pussy Galore (played by Honor Blackman) take cover or conceal themselves. Look for descriptions of any objects they use for concealment, paying particular attention to the colors of these objects. Search multiple sources including movie databases (IMDb, Wikipedia), film reviews, plot summaries, and James Bond fan sites to ensure accuracy of the color details.

**Use Cases**:
- Film archive metadata tagging and color-based object recognition for streaming platforms to improve searchability of classic James Bond scenes
- Auction house prop verification and provenance research by extracting detailed descriptions (color, object type) of memorabilia from historical film endings
- Academic film studies research to analyze gendered concealment tactics and color symbolism in 1960s spy movies using automated search and keyword extraction
- Pop culture blog automation for generating in-depth scene breakdowns of iconic movie finales (e.g., Goldfinger) highlighting props and color details
- Guided tour content creation for movie location tours (e.g., Fort Knox) incorporating narrative of final scenes and specific object/color references
- Trivia app question generation focusing on memorable film details (e.g., color of the parachute James Bond hides under) by scraping multiple online sources
- Museum exhibit cataloging of cinematic artifacts, using color and object data extraction to curate displays on 1960s espionage film memorabilia
- Marketing analysis for product placement impact in classic films, identifying mentions of branded or colored props (parachutes, vehicles) in final scenes

```
import os
import re
import requests

# Search for detailed information about the ending of the 1964 James Bond film 'Goldfinger'
# Focus on the final scenes where Bond and Pussy Galore take cover or conceal themselves
# Look for descriptions of any objects they use for concealment, especially colors

query = 'Goldfinger 1964 James Bond ending final scene Sean Connery Pussy Galore Honor Blackman conceal cover objects colors'
max_results = 15
type = "search"

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print(f"Searching Google for: {query}")
print(f"Max results: {max_results}")
print(f"Search type: {type}")
print("Focus: Final scenes with concealment objects and their colors")

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": max_results,
"type": type,
}

# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
print("\nSearch request successful!")

# Save raw results to workspace for inspection
import json
with open('workspace/goldfinger_ending_search1.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"Raw search results saved to: workspace/goldfinger_ending_search1.json")

# Process and display results
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"\nFound {len(results['organic_results'])} organic search results:")
print("=" * 80)

for i, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"\nResult {i}:")
print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"URL: {link}")
print(f"Snippet: {snippet}")

# Check for relevant keywords in title and snippet
combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower()

# Look for ending/final scene keywords
ending_keywords = ['ending', 'final', 'last', 'conclusion', 'climax', 'finale']
found_ending = [kw for kw in ending_keywords if kw in combined_text]

# Look for concealment/cover keywords
concealment_keywords = ['cover', 'hide', 'conceal', 'behind', 'under', 'parachute', 'shelter']
found_concealment = [kw for kw in concealment_keywords if kw in combined_text]

# Look for color keywords
color_keywords = ['gold', 'golden', 'yellow', 'orange', 'red', 'blue', 'green', 'white', 'black', 'silver', 'color', 'colored']
found_colors = [kw for kw in color_keywords if kw in combined_text]

# Look for character names
character_keywords = ['bond', 'james', 'sean connery', 'pussy galore', 'honor blackman', 'honour blackman']
found_characters = [kw for kw in character_keywords if kw in combined_text]

if found_ending:
print(f"*** ENDING KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_ending)} ***")

if found_concealment:
print(f"*** CONCEALMENT KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_concealment)} ***")

if found_colors:
print(f"*** COLOR KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_colors)} ***")

if found_characters:
print(f"*** CHARACTER KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_characters)} ***")

# Look for specific objects mentioned in the snippet
object_patterns = [
r'parachute',
r'plane',
r'aircraft',
r'Fort Knox',
r'helicopter',
r'escape',
r'rescue'
]

for pattern in object_patterns:
if re.search(pattern, combined_text, re.IGNORECASE):
print(f"*** RELEVANT OBJECT FOUND: {pattern} ***")

# Look for specific descriptions of the ending
ending_patterns = [
r'final scene',
r'ending.*Bond',
r'Pussy Galore.*ending',
r'parachute.*color',
r'golden.*parachute',
r'Fort Knox.*ending'
]

for pattern in ending_patterns:
matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text, re.IGNORECASE)
if matches:
print(f"*** ENDING DESCRIPTION PATTERN: {pattern} -> {matches} ***")

print("-" * 60)
else:
print("\nNo organic search results found.")
else:
print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")

print("\nInitial search for Goldfinger ending completed.")
print("Results saved to workspace for further analysis.")
print("\nNext steps:")
print("1. Analyze the search results for IMDb, Wikipedia, or Bond fan sites")
print("2. Look for specific mentions of parachute colors or concealment objects")
print("3. Conduct more targeted searches if needed")

from ddgs import DDGS import json import os # Since SerpAPI is having connectivity issues, let's use DuckDuckGo search as an alternative # Search for information about Maya Ali's lead role in a romantic action comedy film # directed by Ahsan Rahim and produced by Six Sigma Entertainment print("=== MAYA ALI FILM SEARCH - USING DUCKDUCKGO ===\n") print("Searching for Maya Ali's lead role in romantic action comedy directed by Ahsan Rahim") print("Focus: Six Sigma Entertainment production, gangster marriage plot, 500+ million PKR box office\n") # First search: Comprehensive search with all key elements query1 = "Maya Ali Ahsan Rahim Six Sigma Entertainment romantic action comedy gangster marriage" max_results = 15 region = "en-us" backend = ["google", "duckduckgo", "yandex", "brave", "bing", "yahoo", "mojeek"] print(f"Search Query 1: {query1}") print(f"Max results: {max_results}") print(f"Search backends: {backend}\n") try: searcher = DDGS(timeout=10) results1 = searcher.text(query1, max_results=max_results, page=1, backend=backend, safesearch="off", region=region) if results1 == []: print(f"No results found for query 1: '{query1}'") else: print(f"Found {len(results1)} results for query 1") # Save results to workspace with open('workspace/maya_ali_search1_ddg.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results1, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print("Results saved to: workspace/maya_ali_search1_ddg.json\n") # Analyze results for key information print("=== ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS 1 ===\n") for i, result in enumerate(results1, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f"Result {i}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"URL: {url}") print(f"Description: {body}") # Check for relevant keywords combined_text = f"{title} {body}".lower() # Look for key people people_keywords = ['maya ali', 'ahsan rahim', 'six sigma'] found_people = [kw for kw in people_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Look for genre keywords genre_keywords = ['romantic', 'action', 'comedy', 'rom-com', 'romance'] found_genres = [kw for kw in genre_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Look for plot keywords plot_keywords = ['gangster', 'marriage', 'arranged', 'wedding', 'criminal', 'mafia'] found_plot = [kw for kw in plot_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Look for box office keywords box_office_keywords = ['500 million', '50 crore', 'box office', 'collection', 'earnings', 'pkr', 'rupees'] found_box_office = [kw for kw in box_office_keywords if kw in combined_text] # After "movie" ] for pattern in title_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text) if matches: # Filter meaningful matches filtered_matches = [m.strip() for m in matches if len(m.strip()) > 3] if filtered_matches: print(f"*** POTENTIAL FILM TITLES: {filtered_matches} ***") print("-" * 70) except Exception as e: print(f"Error with search 1: {e}") results1 = [] print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("CONDUCTING SECOND TARGETED SEARCH") print("=" * 80) # from ddgs import DDGS import json import os # Since SerpAPI is having connectivity issues, let's use DuckDuckGo search as an alternative # Search for information about Maya Ali's lead role in a romantic action comedy film # directed by Ahsan Rahim and produced by Six Sigma Entertainment print("=== MAYA ALI FILM SEARCH - USING DUCKDUCKGO ===\n") print("Searching for Maya Ali's lead role in romantic action comedy directed by Ahsan Rahim") print("Focus: Six Sigma Entertainment production, gangster marriage plot, 500+ million PKR box office\n") # First search: Comprehensive search with all key elements query1 = "Maya Ali Ahsan Rahim Six Sigma Entertainment romantic action comedy gangster marriage" max_results = 15 region = "en-us" backend = ["google", "duckduckgo", "yandex", "brave", "bing", "yahoo", "mojeek"] print(f"Search Query 1: {query1}") print(f"Max results: {max_results}") print(f"Search backends: {backend}\n") try: searcher = DDGS(timeout=10) results1 = searcher.text(query1, max_results=max_results, page=1, backend=backend, safesearch="off", region=region) if results1 == []: print(f"No results found for query 1: '{query1}'") else: print(f"Found {len(results1)} results for query 1") # Save results to workspace with open('workspace/maya_ali_search1_ddg.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results1, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print("Results saved to: workspace/maya_ali_search1_ddg.json\n") # Analyze results for key information print("=== ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS 1 ===\n") for i, result in enumerate(results1, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f"Result {i}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"URL: {url}") print(f"Description: {body}") # Check for relevant keywords combined_text = f"{title} {body}".lower() # Look for key people people_keywords = ['maya ali', 'ahsan rahim', 'six sigma'] found_people = [kw for kw in people_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Look for genre keywords genre_keywords = ['romantic', 'action', 'comedy', 'rom-com', 'romance'] found_genres = [kw for kw in genre_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Look for plot keywords plot_keywords = ['gangster', 'marriage', 'arranged', 'wedding', 'criminal', 'mafia'] found_plot = [kw for kw in plot_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Look for box office keywords box_office_keywords = ['500 million', '50 crore', 'box office', 'collection', 'earnings', 'pkr', 'rupees'] found_box_office = [kw for kw in box_office_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Look for Pakistani film indicators pakistani_indicators = ['lollywood', 'pakistani film', 'karachi', 'lahore', 'urdu film', 'punjabi film', 'pakistan'] found_pakistani = [kw for kw in pakistani_indicators if kw in combined_text] if found_people: print(f"*** KEY PEOPLE FOUND: {', '.join(found_people)} ***") if found_genres: print(f"*** GENRE KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_genres)} ***") if found_plot: print(f"*** PLOT KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_plot)} ***") if found_box_office: print(f"*** BOX OFFICE KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_box_office)} ***") if found_pakistani: print(f"*** PAKISTANI FILM INDICATORS: {', '.join(found_pakistani)} ***") # Look for potential film titles in quotes or specific patterns import re title_patterns = [ r'"([^"]+)"', # Text in double quotes r"'([^']+)'", # Text in single quotes r'film\s+([A-Z][a-zA-Z\s]+)', # After "film" r'movie\s+([A-Z][a-zA-Z\s]+)', # After "movie" ] for pattern in title_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text) if matches: # Filter meaningful matches filtered_matches = [m.strip() for m in matches if len(m.strip()) > 3] if filtered_matches: print(f"*** POTENTIAL FILM TITLES: {filtered_matches} ***") print("-" * 70) except Exception as e: print(f"Error with search 1: {e}") results1 = [] print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("CONDUCTING SECOND TARGETED SEARCH") print("=" * 80) # Second search: Focus on Maya Ali Pakistani films with box office success query2 = "Maya Ali Pakistani film 500 million PKR box office romantic comedy" print(f"\nSearch Query 2: {query2}") print("Focus: Pakistani films with Maya Ali that earned high box office collections\n") try: results2 = searcher.text(query2, max_results=max_results, page=1, backend=backend, safesearch="off", region=region) if results2 == []: print(f"No results found for query 2: '{query2}'") else: print(f"Found {len(results2)} results for query 2") # Save results to workspace with open('workspace/maya_ali_search2_ddg.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results2, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print("Results saved to: workspace/maya_ali_search2_ddg.json\n") # Check for specific film mentions combined_text = f"{title} {body}".lower() # Look for Maya Ali specifically if 'maya ali' in combined_text: print("*** MAYA ALI MENTIONED ***") # Look for box office numbers import re box_office_patterns = [ r'(\d+)\s*million', r'(\d+)\s*crore', r'pkr\s*(\d+)', r'rs\.?\s*(\d+)', r'rupees\s*(\d+)' ] for pattern in box_office_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text) if matches: print(f"*** BOX OFFICE NUMBERS FOUND: {matches} ***") # Look for film titles mentioned with Maya Ali if 'maya ali' in combined_text: # Extract potential film titles near Maya Ali mentions maya_context = combined_text film_keywords = ['film', 'movie', 'cinema', 'picture'] for keyword in film_keywords: if keyword in maya_context: print(f"*** FILM CONTEXT WITH MAYA ALI: Contains '{keyword}' ***") print("-" * 70) except Exception as e: print(f"Error with search 2: {e}") results2 = [] print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("CONDUCTING THIRD TARGETED SEARCH") print("=" * 80) # Six Sigma Entertainment as producer # 2. 500+ million PKR box office performance print("=== FOCUSED VERIFICATION SEARCH FOR TEEFA IN TROUBLE ===\n") print("Target Film: Teefa in Trouble (2018)") print("Remaining verification needed:") print("- Six Sigma Entertainment as producer") print("- 500+ million PKR box office collection\n") # Search 1: Focus on Teefa in Trouble production details and Six Sigma Entertainment query1 = "Teefa in Trouble 2018 Six Sigma Entertainment producer production company" max_results = 15 region = "en-us" backend = ["google", "duckduckgo", "yandex", "brave", "bing", "yahoo", "mojeek"] print(f"Search Query 1: {query1}") print("Focus: Production company and producer details\n") try: searcher = DDGS(timeout=10) results1 = searcher.text(query1, max_results=max_results, page=1, backend=backend, safesearch="off", region=region) if results1 == []: print(f"No results found for query 1: '{query1}'") else: print(f"Found {len(results1)} results for production search") # Save results to workspace with open('workspace/teefa_production_search.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results1, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print("Results saved to: workspace/teefa_production_search.json\n") print("=== ANALYZING PRODUCTION SEARCH RESULTS ===\n") for i, result in enumerate(results1, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f"Result {i}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"URL: {url}") print(f"Description: {body}") # Check for key information combined_text = f"{title} {body}".lower() # Look for Six Sigma Entertainment if 'six sigma' in combined_text: print("*** SIX SIGMA ENTERTAINMENT MENTIONED ***") if 'teefa' in combined_text: print("*** DIRECT CONNECTION TO TEEFA IN TROUBLE ***") # Look for production company details production_keywords = ['producer', 'production', 'company', 'banner', 'entertainment'] found_production = [kw for kw in production_keywords if kw in combined_text] if found_production: print(f"*** PRODUCTION KEYWORDS: {', '.join(found_production)} ***") # Look for other production companies mentioned if 'lightingale' in combined_text or 'tadpole' in combined_text: print("*** OTHER PRODUCTION COMPANIES MENTIONED ***") print("-" * 70) except Exception as e: print(f"Error with production search: {e}") results1 = [] print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("SEARCH 2: BOX OFFICE PERFORMANCE") print("=" * 80) # Save results to workspace with open('workspace/teefa_boxoffice_search.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results2, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print("Results saved to: workspace/teefa_boxoffice_search.json\n") print("=== ANALYZING BOX OFFICE SEARCH RESULTS ===\n") for i, result in enumerate(results2, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f"Result {i}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"URL: {url}") print(f"Description: {body}") combined_text = f"{title} {body}".lower() # Look for box office numbers import re box_office_patterns = [ r'(\d+)\s*million.*pkr', r'(\d+)\s*crore', r'pkr\s*(\d+)', r'rs\.?\s*(\d+)\s*million', r'(\d+)\s*million.*rupees', r'500\s*million', r'50\s*crore' ] box_office_found = False for pattern in box_office_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text, re.IGNORECASE) if matches: print(f"*** BOX OFFICE NUMBERS FOUND: {matches} (Pattern: {pattern}) ***") box_office_found = True # Look for box office keywords box_office_keywords = ['box office', 'collection', 'earnings', 'grossed', 'revenue', 'hit', 'blockbuster', 'success'] found_box_office = [kw for kw in box_office_keywords if kw in combined_text] if found_box_office: print(f"*** BOX OFFICE KEYWORDS: {', '.join(found_box_office)} ***") # Search 1: Focus on Teefa in Trouble production details and Six Sigma Entertainment query1 = "Teefa in Trouble 2018 Six Sigma Entertainment producer production company" max_results = 15 region = "en-us" backend = ["google", "duckduckgo", "yandex", "brave", "bing", "yahoo", "mojeek"] print(f"Search Query 1: {query1}") print("Focus: Production company and producer details\n") try: searcher = DDGS(timeout=10) results1 = searcher.text(query1, max_results=max_results, page=1, backend=backend, safesearch="off", region=region) if results1 == []: print(f"No results found for query 1: '{query1}'") else: print(f"Found {len(results1)} results for production search") # Save results to workspace with open('workspace/teefa_production_search.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results1, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print("Results saved to: workspace/teefa_production_search.json\n") print("=== ANALYZING PRODUCTION SEARCH RESULTS ===\n") for i, result in enumerate(results1, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') body = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f"Result {i}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"URL: {url}") print(f"Description: {body}") # Check for key information combined_text = f"{title} {body}".lower() # Look for Six Sigma Entertainment if 'six sigma' in combined_text: print("*** SIX SIGMA ENTERTAINMENT MENTIONED ***") if 'teefa' in combined_text: print("*** DIRECT CONNECTION TO TEEFA IN TROUBLE ***") # Look for production company details production_keywords = ['producer', 'production', 'company', 'banner', 'entertainment'] found_production = [kw for kw in production_keywords if kw in combined_text] if found_production: print(f"*** PRODUCTION KEYWORDS: {', '.join(found_production)} ***") # Look for other production companies mentioned if 'lightingale' in combined_text or 'tadpole' in combined_text: print("*** OTHER PRODUCTION COMPANIES MENTIONED ***") print("-" * 70) except Exception as e: print(f"Error with production search: {e}") results1 = [] print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("SEARCH 2: BOX OFFICE PERFORMANCE") print("=" * 80) # Look for box office numbers import re box_office_patterns = [ r'(\d+)\s*million.*pkr', r'(\d+)\s*crore', r'pkr\s*(\d+)', r'rs\.?\s*(\d+)\s*million', r'(\d+)\s*million.*rupees', r'500\s*million', r'50\s*crore' ] box_office_found = False for pattern in box_office_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text, re.IGNORECASE) if matches: print(f"*** BOX OFFICE NUMBERS FOUND: {matches} (Pattern: {pattern}) ***") box_office_found = True # - Entertainment database enrichment and automated character role extraction for actor profiles in online movie encyclopedias
- Journalism fact-checking of actor filmography details and character roles when preparing articles on Polish television series
- Academic film studies research and metadata gathering for analyzing casting patterns in early-2000s TV dramas

- Archival library cataloging and verification of cast roles in historical television productions for media heritage projects

```
import os
import re
import requests

# Search for information about Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski's role in 'Magda M.'
query = 'Bart≈Çomiej Kasprzykowski Magda M. cast character role'
max_results = 15
type = "search"

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print(f"Searching Google for: {query}")
print(f"Max results: {max_results}")
print(f"Search type: {type}")

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": max_results,
"type": type,
}

# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
print("\nSearch request successful!")

# Save raw results to workspace for inspection
import json
with open('workspace/kasprzykowski_magda_m_search_results.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"Raw search results saved to: workspace/kasprzykowski_magda_m_search_results.json")

# Process and display results
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"\nFound {len(results['organic_results'])} organic search results:")
print("=" * 60)

for i, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"\nResult {i}:")
print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"URL: {link}")
print(f"Snippet: {snippet}")

# Check for relevant keywords in title and snippet
combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower()
relevant_keywords = ['kasprzykowski', 'magda m', 'cast', 'character', 'role', 'actor', 'film', 'series']
found_keywords = [kw for kw in relevant_keywords if kw in combined_text]

if found_keywords:
print(f"*** RELEVANT KEYWORDS FOUND: {', '.join(found_keywords)} ***")

# Look for potential character names in snippets
# Common patterns: "plays [character]", "as [character]", "role of [character]"
character_patterns = [
r'plays?\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'as\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'role\s+of\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'character\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'wcieli≈Ç\s+siƒô\s+w\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
r'gra\s+([A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+(?:\s+[A-ZƒÑƒÜƒò≈Å≈É√ì≈ö≈π≈ª][a-zƒÖƒáƒô≈Ç≈Ñ√≥≈õ≈∫≈º]+)*)',
]

for pattern in character_patterns:
matches = re.findall(pattern, combined_text, re.IGNORECASE)
if matches:
print(f"*** POTENTIAL CHARACTER NAME(S) FOUND: {matches} ***")

print("-" * 40)
else:
print("\nNo organic search results found.")
else:

analysis_results['death_information'].extend(death_info_found)
else:
print('‚ùì No direct death information found in sentences with Chen Boda')

# Look for year patterns (1900-2025)
year_pattern = re.compile(r'\b(19\d{2}|20[0-2]\d)\b')
years_found = year_pattern.findall(page_text)

if years_found:
year_counts = Counter(years_found)
print(f'üìÖ Years mentioned: {dict(year_counts.most_common(10))}')

# Look for years near death-related words
potential_death_years = []
for year in set(years_found):
for death_word in death_keywords[:5]: # Check main English death words
# Find positions of year and death word
year_positions = [m.start() for m in re.finditer(year, page_text)]
death_positions = [m.start() for m in re.finditer(death_word, page_text_lower)]

for year_pos in year_positions:
for death_pos in death_positions:
distance = abs(year_pos - death_pos)
if distance < 200: # Within 200 characters
context_start = max(0, min(year_pos, death_pos) - 50)
context_end = max(year_pos, death_pos) + 100
context = page_text[context_start:context_end]
potential_death_years.append({
'year': year,
'death_word': death_word,
'distance': distance,
'context': context.strip()
})

if potential_death_years:
print(f'üéØ Potential death years found: {len(potential_death_years)}')
# Sort by distance (closer = more likely)
potential_death_years.sort(key=lambda x: x['distance'])
for death_year in potential_death_years[:3]: # Show top 3
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {death_year["year"]} (near "{death_year["death_word"]}", distance: {death_year["distance"]} chars)')
print(f' Context: {death_year["context"][:150]}...')
analysis_results['potential_death_years'].extend(potential_death_years)

analysis_results['year_mentions'].extend(years_found)
else:
print('‚ùì No years found in this file')

# Look for biographical information (CRITICAL FIX: sentence_lower as first line)
bio_keywords = ['born', 'birth', 'biography', 'biographical', 'life', 'career', 'Âá∫Áîü', 'ÁîüÂπ≥', '‰º†ËÆ∞']
bio_info = []

for keyword in bio_keywords:
if keyword in page_text_lower or keyword in page_text: # Check both for Chinese
sentences = re.split(r'[.!?„ÄÇÔºÅÔºü]', page_text)
for sentence in sentences:
# CRITICAL FIX: Define sentence_lower as the FIRST line in the loop
sentence_lower = sentence.lower()

if (keyword in sentence_lower or keyword in sentence) and len(sentence.strip()) > 15:
if any(indicator in sentence_lower or indicator in sentence for indicator in chen_boda_indicators.keys()):
bio_info.append({
'keyword': keyword,
'sentence': sentence.strip()[:250]
})
break

if bio_info:
print(f'üìñ Biographical information found: {len(bio_info)} instances')
for info in bio_info[:2]: # Show first 2
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {info["keyword"]}: {info["sentence"]}...')
analysis_results['biographical_data'].extend(bio_info)
else:
print('‚ùì No biographical information found')

# Store Chen Boda mention info
analysis_results['chen_boda_mentions'].append({
'filename': filename,
'mentions': chen_boda_indicators,
'total_mentions': total_mentions,
'death_info_count': len(death_info_found),
'bio_info_count': len(bio_info),
'years_found': len(years_found) if years_found else 0,
'potential_death_years': len(potential_death_years) if potential_death_years else 0
})

else:
print('‚ùå No Chen Boda mentions found in this file')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error analyzing {filename}: {str(e)}')

print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('COMPREHENSIVE CHEN BODA DEATH YEAR ANALYSIS SUMMARY')
print('=' * 80)

# Summarize findings
total_chen_boda_mentions = sum(mention['total_mentions'] for mention in analysis_results['chen_boda_mentions'])
total_death_info = len(analysis_results['death_information'])
total_bio_info = len(analysis_results['biographical_data'])
total_potential_death_years = len(analysis_results['potential_death_years'])

print(f'üìä ANALYSIS SUMMARY:')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Files analyzed: {analysis_results["files_analyzed"]}')

print(f' ‚Ä¢ Biographical information instances: {total_bio_info}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Potential death years identified: {total_potential_death_years}')

# Analyze potential death years
if analysis_results['potential_death_years']:
print(f'\nüíÄ DEATH YEAR ANALYSIS:')

print('Most frequently mentioned years near death-related terms:')
for year, count in death_year_counts.most_common(5):

# Show best death year candidates
print(f'\nüéØ BEST DEATH YEAR CANDIDATES:')
# Sort by proximity to death words (smaller distance = better)
sorted_candidates = sorted(analysis_results['potential_death_years'], key=lambda x: x['distance'])

for i, candidate in enumerate(sorted_candidates[:5], 1):
print(f'\n{i}. YEAR: {candidate["year"]} (Distance: {candidate["distance"]} characters from "{candidate["death_word"]}")')

if total_death_info > 0: confidence_score += 30
if total_potential_death_years > 0: confidence_score += 25
if total_bio_info > 0: confidence_score += 15

print(f' Confidence level: {confidence_score}/100')
else:

print('‚ö†Ô∏è MODERATE EVIDENCE FOUND:')

if analysis_results['potential_death_years']:

most_likely = death_year_counts.most_common(1)[0]

if mention['death_info_count'] > 0:
print(f' - Death info instances: {mention["death_info_count"]}')
if mention['bio_info_count'] > 0:
print(f' - Bio info instances: {mention["bio_info_count"]}')
if mention['years_found'] > 0:
print(f' - Years found: {mention["years_found"]}')
if mention['potential_death_years'] > 0:
print(f' - Potential death years: {mention["potential_death_years"]}')

# Final recommendation based on findings
print(f'\nüéØ FINAL RECOMMENDATION:')
if total_potential_death_years > 0:
death_year_counts = Counter([item['year'] for item in analysis_results['potential_death_years']])
most_common_year = death_year_counts.most_common(1)[0][0]
print(f'Based on search result analysis, Chen Boda most likely died in {most_common_year}')
print(f'This conclusion is based on {total_potential_death_years} contextual mentions')
print(f'near death-related terms in the retrieved search results.')
elif total_chen_boda_mentions > 0:
print('While Chen Boda content was found in search results, specific death')
print('year information was not clearly identified. Historical records suggest')
print('Chen Boda died in 1989, but this requires verification from additional sources.')
else:
print('No Chen Boda content found in current search results.')
print('Recommend trying different search terms or sources.')

print('\n=== CHEN BODA DEATH YEAR ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===')

### Development Step 13: Locate and Confirm Chen Boda‚Äôs Death Year from Reliable Biographical Sources

**Description**: Search for the death year of Chen Boda, who was born in Hui'an County, Fujian Province (a region known for China's national intangible cultural heritage stone carving techniques), authored extensive critiques against Chiang Kai-shek's political works, and served as Mao Zedong's chief interpreter and ghostwriter. Focus on finding reliable biographical information about Chen Boda's death date, including searches for 'Chen Boda death year', 'Chen Boda biography died', and 'Chen Boda Èôà‰ºØËææ death date'. Cross-reference multiple sources to confirm the exact year of his death.

**Use Cases**:
- Genealogy research automation for family historians: extracting and verifying death dates of ancestors from digitized local archives and memorial websites.
- Historical archive metadata enrichment for librarians: automatically identifying and updating death year fields in digital collections of political figures‚Äô biographies.
- Academic research on political elite longevity: aggregating and cross-referencing death years of mid-20th century Chinese leaders to study lifespan patterns.
- Journalistic fact-checking for obituary writing: quickly confirming the death date of prominent figures by scanning saved news article HTML and authoritative biographical sources.
- Educational publishing timeline validation: ensuring history textbook publishers have accurate death years for Mao Zedong‚Äôs inner circle when compiling political chronology.
- Cultural heritage database curation: verifying biographical details (including death year) of practitioners in regional stone carving traditions to maintain national intangible cultural heritage records.
- Compliance due-diligence in international partnerships: risk analysts confirming the life status and death information of prospective foreign business associates with politically sensitive backgrounds.
