from ddgs import DDGS import json import os from datetime import datetime print('=== MAYA ALI BIRTH YEAR SEARCH - COMPREHENSIVE APPROACH ===') print('Searching for Pakistani actress Maya Ali\'s birth year and biographical information\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists workspace_dir = 'workspace' if not os.path.exists(workspace_dir): os.makedirs(workspace_dir) print(f'Created workspace directory: {workspace_dir}') # Initialize search results storage search_results = { 'target_person': 'Maya Ali (Pakistani actress)', 'objective': 'Find birth year and date of birth information', 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'queries': [], 'results': [], 'biographical_data': [], 'birth_info_found': [] } # Define multiple search queries for comprehensive coverage search_queries = [ 'Maya Ali Pakistani actress birth year date of birth biography', 'Maya Ali actress Pakistan born when age biography', 'Maya Ali Pakistani drama actress personal information birth date', 'Maya Ali actress biography filmography birth year Pakistan', 'Maya Ali born date of birth Pakistani television actress' ] print(f'üìã EXECUTING {len(search_queries)} TARGETED SEARCHES:') print('=' * 60) # Execute searches using multiple backends searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) backends = ["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yandex", "brave"] for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nüîç Search {i}: {query}') print('-' * 50) try: # Try multiple backends sequentially results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=backends, safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'‚úÖ Found {len(results)} results') # Store query and results search_results['queries'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': len(results), 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() }) # Process and analyze each result for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f' Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title[:80]}...' if len(title) > 80 else f' Title: {title}') print(f' URL: {link}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:120]}...' if len(snippet) > 120 else f' Snippet: {snippet}') # Check for birth-related keywords in title and snippet combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower() birth_keywords = ['born', 'birth', 'age', 'birthday', 'date of birth', 'dob', 'biography', 'bio'] year_pattern = r'\b(19\d{2}|20[0-2]\d)\b' found_keywords = [kw for kw in birth_keywords if kw in combined_text] if found_keywords: print(f' *** BIRTH KEYWORDS FOUND: {", ".join(found_keywords)} ***') # Look for potential birth years import re years_found = re.findall(year_pattern, combined_text) if years_found: print(f' *** POTENTIAL BIRTH YEARS: {", ".join(set(years_found))} ***') # Store result with analysis result_data = { 'query_index': i, 'result_index': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'birth_keywords_found': found_keywords, 'years_mentioned': list(set(years_found)) if years_found else [], 'relevance_score': len(found_keywords) + len(set(years_found)) if years_found else len(found_keywords) } search_results['results'].append(result_data) # If this result seems highly relevant, mark it for detailed analysis if result_data['relevance_score'] >= 2: print(f' üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE SCORE: {result_data["relevance_score"]} - Marked for analysis') search_results['birth_info_found'].append(result_data) print() search_results['results'].extend(results) else: print('‚ùå No results found for this query') search_results['queries'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': 0, 'error': 'No results returned' }) except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error executing search: {str(e)}') search_results['queries'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': 0, 'error': str(e) }) print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('MAYA ALI BIRTH YEAR SEARCH SUMMARY') print('=' * 80) # Analyze all collected results total_results = len([r for r in search_results['results'] if isinstance(r, dict) and 'title' in r]) total_high_relevance = len(search_results['birth_info_found']) successful_queries = len([q for q in search_results['queries'] if q.get('results_count', 0) > 0]) print(f'üìä SEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total queries executed: {len(search_queries)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful queries: {successful_queries}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total results collected: {total_results}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ High relevance results: {total_high_relevance}') # Analyze birth information found if search_results['birth_info_found']: print(f'\nüéØ HIGH RELEVANCE RESULTS ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 50) # Sort by relevance score sorted_results = sorted(search_results['birth_info_found'], key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) for i, result in enumerate(sorted_results[:5], 1): # Show top 5 print(f'\n{i}. RELEVANCE SCORE: {result["relevance_score"]}') print(f' Title: {result["title"]}') print(f' URL: {result["link"]}') print(f' Snippet: {result["snippet"]}') print(f' Birth keywords: {", ".join(result["birth_keywords_found"])}') if result['years_mentioned']: print(f' Years mentioned: {", ".join(result["years_mentioned"])}') print(f' Source query: {search_queries[result["query_index"]-1]}') # Collect all years mentioned across high-relevance results all_years = [] for result in search_results['birth_info_found']: all_years.extend(result['years_mentioned']) if all_years: from collections import Counter year_counts = Counter(all_years) print(f'\nüìÖ BIRTH YEAR ANALYSIS:') print('Most frequently mentioned years in high-relevance results:') for year, count in year_counts.most_common(5): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {year}: mentioned {count} time(s)') # Determine most likely birth year if year_counts: most_likely_year = year_counts.most_common(1)[0] print(f'\nüèÜ MOST LIKELY BIRTH YEAR: {most_likely_year[0]} (mentioned {most_likely_year[1]} time(s))') search_results['most_likely_birth_year'] = most_likely_year[0] search_results['birth_year_confidence'] = most_likely_year[1] else: print('\n‚ùì No high-relevance birth information found in search results') print(' Recommend manual review of search results or additional targeted searches') # Save comprehensive search results results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'maya_ali_birth_search_results.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Show final summary print(f'\n' + '=' * 80) print('FINAL MAYA ALI BIRTH YEAR SEARCH CONCLUSION') print('=' * 80) if 'most_likely_birth_year' in search_results: print(f'‚úÖ SUCCESS: Maya Ali\'s most likely birth year is {search_results["most_likely_birth_year"]}') print(f'üìà Confidence: Based on {search_results["birth_year_confidence"]} mention(s) in high-relevance sources') print(f'üìã Evidence: Found in {total_high_relevance} high-relevance search results') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è PARTIAL SUCCESS: Search completed but birth year requires manual verification') print(f'üìã Data collected: {total_results} search results from {successful_queries} successful queries') print('üîç Next step: Manual review of collected search results for birth information') print(f'\nüìÅ All search data saved to workspace for further analysis') print('=== MAYA ALI BIRTH YEAR SEARCH COMPLETE ===')
